class=\char`\"{}panel-\/body\char`\"{}$>$ Throughout this document, we use index notation \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_ad82b3af3f60293545ff52365c15128e9}{and}} write, e.\+g., \textbackslash{}f\$ \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_a815c7caeb20923220296c8663a500a05}{u}}(x\+\_\+1, x\+\_\+2) \textbackslash{}f\$ as \textbackslash{}f\$ \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_a815c7caeb20923220296c8663a500a05}{u}}(\mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_a69f138496db3ebde4b24d470abde0964}{x\+\_\+i}}) \textbackslash{}f\$. We do not explicitly state \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_af1f17d1d5290c89ad5e65300b710dbd7}{the}} range of free indices where it is clear from \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_af1f17d1d5290c89ad5e65300b710dbd7}{the}} context -\/-\/ in \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_af1f17d1d5290c89ad5e65300b710dbd7}{the}} above example it would be equal \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_a50ca6d8f78e851220d6bafe6cad4aa50}{to}} \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_af1f17d1d5290c89ad5e65300b710dbd7}{the}} spatial dimension of \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_af1f17d1d5290c89ad5e65300b710dbd7}{the}} problem. All mathematical derivations are presented using \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_af1f17d1d5290c89ad5e65300b710dbd7}{the}} \char`\"{}natural\char`\"{} numbering of \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_af1f17d1d5290c89ad5e65300b710dbd7}{the}} indices\+:e.\+g., \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_af1f17d1d5290c89ad5e65300b710dbd7}{the}} components of \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_af1f17d1d5290c89ad5e65300b710dbd7}{the}} 3D vector \textbackslash{}f\$\{\textbackslash{}bf \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_a886ef2b0d224d9e63aec0b2a6870be2c}{f}}\}\textbackslash{}f\$ are \textbackslash{}f\$ f\+\_\+1, f\+\_\+2 \textbackslash{}f\$ \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_ad82b3af3f60293545ff52365c15128e9}{and}} \textbackslash{}f\$ f\+\_\+3 \textbackslash{}f\$. Unfortunately, this notation is inconsistent with \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_af1f17d1d5290c89ad5e65300b710dbd7}{the}} implementation of vectors(\mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_ad82b3af3f60293545ff52365c15128e9}{and}} most other standard \char`\"{}containers\char`\"{}) in C++where \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_af1f17d1d5290c89ad5e65300b710dbd7}{the}} indices start from 0 \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_ad82b3af3f60293545ff52365c15128e9}{and}} \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_af1f17d1d5290c89ad5e65300b710dbd7}{the}} components of \textbackslash{}c vector$<$ double $>$ \textbackslash{}c \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_a886ef2b0d224d9e63aec0b2a6870be2c}{f}}(3) are \textbackslash{}c \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_a886ef2b0d224d9e63aec0b2a6870be2c}{f}}\mbox{[}0\mbox{]}, \textbackslash{}c \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_a886ef2b0d224d9e63aec0b2a6870be2c}{f}}\mbox{[}1\mbox{]} \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_ad82b3af3f60293545ff52365c15128e9}{and}} \textbackslash{}c \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_a886ef2b0d224d9e63aec0b2a6870be2c}{f}}\mbox{[}2\mbox{]}. There is no elegant way \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_a50ca6d8f78e851220d6bafe6cad4aa50}{to}} resolve this conflict. Adopting C++-\/style numbering in \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_af1f17d1d5290c89ad5e65300b710dbd7}{the}} theoretical development would make \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_af1f17d1d5290c89ad5e65300b710dbd7}{the}} mathematics look very odd(try it!)

\mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_a3f06ee645524112cd97f921e588d9ce3}{A}} note on notation$<$/B$>$ $<$/C\+E\+N\+T\+ER$>$ $<$div class=\char`\"{}panel-\/body\char`\"{}$>$ Throughout this document, we use index notation \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_ad82b3af3f60293545ff52365c15128e9}{and}} write, e.\+g., \textbackslash{}f\$ We do not explicitly state \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_af1f17d1d5290c89ad5e65300b710dbd7}{the}} range of free indices where it is clear from \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_af1f17d1d5290c89ad5e65300b710dbd7}{the}} context -\/-\/ in \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_af1f17d1d5290c89ad5e65300b710dbd7}{the}} above example it would be equal \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_a50ca6d8f78e851220d6bafe6cad4aa50}{to}} \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_af1f17d1d5290c89ad5e65300b710dbd7}{the}} spatial dimension of \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_af1f17d1d5290c89ad5e65300b710dbd7}{the}} problem. All mathematical derivations are presented using \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_af1f17d1d5290c89ad5e65300b710dbd7}{the}} \char`\"{}natural\char`\"{} numbering of \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_af1f17d1d5290c89ad5e65300b710dbd7}{the}} indices\+: e.\+g., \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_af1f17d1d5290c89ad5e65300b710dbd7}{the}} components of \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_af1f17d1d5290c89ad5e65300b710dbd7}{the}} 3D vector \textbackslash{}f\$\{\textbackslash{}bf \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_a886ef2b0d224d9e63aec0b2a6870be2c}{f}}\}\textbackslash{}f\$ are \textbackslash{}f\$ f\+\_\+1, f\+\_\+2 \textbackslash{}f\$ \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_ad82b3af3f60293545ff52365c15128e9}{and}} \textbackslash{}f\$ f\+\_\+3 \textbackslash{}f\$. There is no elegant way \mbox{\hyperlink{intro_8txt_a50ca6d8f78e851220d6bafe6cad4aa50}{to}} resolve this conflict.
